 - Offer white sandalwood and yellow and white flowers to mother Saraswati with right hand
 - kesar mishrit kheer arpit karnaa sarvottam hoga
 - It will be best to chant the basic mantra of Maa Saraswati
 - kaale, nile kapadon kaa prayog pujan main bhuulakar bhi naa karen

 vidya main man nahin lag paata he or pratispardhaa main bhi safal nahin ho pate hai

 - brihaspati ke kamjor hone par vidya prapti main baadha ke saath-saath vivaah or daampaty jivan me bhi mushkilen aane lagati hai

 These youths beat up many people, including children and women
 iske baad dabang saream pistaul tanakar dhamkee dete hue faraar ho gayi
 Later on receiving information about the incident, the police reached the spot and took into custody the three youths named
 maamle kii gambhirtha ko dekhte hue jila varisht police adheekshak balavaan singh rana evam atirikt upayukta jaibir singh arya maukey par pahunche or sthiti kaa jayja liya
 The top officials have assured to provide full protection to the victims, take strict action against the accused, compensate the damage caused by the sabotage and get the injured treated at government expense
 suraksha kii drushti se gaanv main police bal tainaat kiya gaya he
 According to sources, two young men of Manjit's family who were injured by the beating of the bullies, Satish and Budhraj, went for a bath on the canal outside the village by bike
 vahaan par gaanv kilajafargarh nivasee dabang samudaay ke yuvakon ne unki bike chhinane kaa prayaas kiya
 Meanwhile, Manjit, who was grazing the cattle in the fields nearby, intervened and sent Satish and Budhraj home and he also came home with the animals
 iske kuch samay baad 10-15 yuvakon ne aakar unke gharon main todphod karne ke saath-saath unki pitayee kar di or faraar ho gayi
 Mumbai Indians, ranked seventh in the table, beat Rajasthan Royals by eight runs at the Wankhede Stadium on Friday in the 32nd match of the Indian Premier League
 mumbai indiens kii is sanskaran main yah teesri jeet he
 The target of 188 runs was to win in front of the Royals but the team could only score 179 runs after losing seven wickets
 mumbai indiens kii ore se 53 ranon kii naabad pari khilne vaale ambati raidu main of da match chune gaye
 However, the Rajasthan Royals got off to a solid start and Ajinkya Rahane (16) added 30 runs for the first wicket with Shane Watson (28) thanks to a live-in from the first over
 rahane kaa kaich pehle over kii paanchavin gend par jagadish suchit ne choda
 In the fourth over, Vinay Kumar showed Rahane the way to the pavilion
 iske baad sanju samson (76) ne watasan ke saath duusare wicket ke liye 41 or phir steven smith (23) ke saath tisare wicket ke liye 56 ranon kii saajhedaari kar royles ummiden kaayam rakhin
 Mitchell mclanegan, however, took two wickets in the 18th over to open the way for the return of Mumbai Indians
 maclengan ne over kii chauthi gend par samson or phir karun nair (7) ko chalata kiya
 In the next over, Lasith Malinga also sent Deepak Hooda (1) to the pavilion, ending the Royals' true expectations
 samson ne 46 gendon kii pari main saat chauke or teen chakke lagaae
 mclennan scored three successes for Mumbai Indians
 malinga, vinay kumaar or suchit ko ek-ek wicket mila
 Earlier, Mumbai Indians scored 187 runs for the loss of five wickets in 20 overs, batting first after losing the toss
 ambati raidu ne 27 gendon main chaar chaukon or teen chhakkon kii madad se naabad 53 ranon kii pari kheli
 Mumbai Indians scored 67 runs in the last five overs thanks to a sharp 61-ball 29-run partnership for the fifth wicket between Kieron Pollard (24) and Ambati Rayudu
 pollard aakhri over main pavilion laute
 Lendl Simmons (38) and Parthiv Patel (23) scored 4 for Mumbai Indians
 5 overon main 43 ranon jodakar team ko acchhee shuruyaat dilaai
 Simmons got a life on the second ball of the match
 tim soudi kii gend par simons ne balla lagaaya or gend wicket ke peeche chali gai
 Wicketkeeper Sanju Samson, however, could not cover it in his glove
 iske baad simons ne mili maukey kaa bharpoor phayda uthaate hue 31 gendon kii pari main chaar chauke or ek chakka lagaaya
 He was dismissed LBW by Ankit Sharma in the 10th over of the innings
 baharhaal, mumbai indiens kaa pehla wicket dhaval kulkarni ne parthiv patel ko apni hi gend par kaich kar hasil kiya
 Patel hit five fours in his 14-ball knock
 tippaniyan Unmukt Chand, who came in third order, contributed only 13 runs
 chand ke pavilion lautne ke baad rohit sharma (27) ne chauthe wicket ke liye raidu ke saath 25 gendon main 36 ran jode
 Dhawal Kulkarni scored two successes from the Royals
 tim soudi, juaan theron or ankit sharma ko ek-ek wicket mila
 Ambati Rayudu was adjudged Man of the Match for Mumbai Indians for his unbeaten innings of 53 runs
 baharhaal, rajasthan royles ko haalanki thos shuruyaat mili or ajinkya rahane (16) ne pehle hi over main mili ek jeevandaan kii badaulat shen watasan (28) ke saath pehle wicket ke liye 30 ran jode
 Rahane catches Jagdish Suchit off the fifth ball of the first over
 chauthe over main vinay kumaar ne rahane ko pavilion kaa rasta dikhaaya
 After this, Sanju Samson (76) kept the Royals hopes by sharing a 41 for the second wicket with Watson and then 56 runs for the third wicket with Steven Smith (23)
 mishael maclengan ne haalanki 18wein over lagaataar do wicket jhatakate hue mumbai indiens kii vaapasi kaa rasta khol diya
 mcclegan drove Samson and then Karun Nair (7) off the fourth ball of the over
 agle over main lasith malinga ne deepak hooda (1) ko bhi pavilion bhej kar royles kii rahi-sahi ummiden khatm kar di

 mumbai indiens kii ore se maclengan ne teen safaltaaen hasil kii

 ise ek saahasik nirnay kaha ja saktaa he, kyonki bharat main ab bhi ge kapal yaa samalangikta ko kanoonee darja hasil nahin he
 However, there is a possibility of this step getting caught in the legal controversy
 saim sex partner kaa matlab he ki yadi koi ge yaa lesbian he to vah apane health insurance ke benifit main apane partner ko bhi jod saktaa he
 Till now the health insurance scheme provided to the employees in the Indian corporate world includes their spouses, children, parents or in-laws
 times of india kii khabar ke mutabik bharat main abhi dhara 377 ke tahat homo sexuality, lesbian, ge, baisexual yaa trans gender sex ko aparaadh mana jaataa he
 Therefore, no such partner is included in any type of insurance plan
 isliye RBS ne yah nirnay liya ki vah saim sex partner ko beemaa suvidha dene kaa kharch khud hi uthayega
 However, it is a matter of thinking that if it is legal to keep such a sex relation or a party then how can this bank give insurance cover to such partner
 isliye aisa lagata he ki yah suvidha kanoonee pachade main bhi funs sakati he
 This policy in the bank will be implemented from the new financial year i
e
 1st April
 abhi tak companiyaan tamaam tarah kii suvidhaayen apane karmchaariyon ko detii rahi hai, lekin yah suvidha pehali baar saamne ai he

 haalanki kai companiyon ne saim sex partner ke liye adopshan live, patternity live, rilokation jaisi suvidhaayen jarur shuru kii thim
 However, the challenge before the companies has been how to do all this within the purview of Indian law, because in India, same sex marriage is not considered valid
 supreme courtne sexual orientation ko jaahir karne kii aazaadee to di he, lekin saim sex relation ko aparaadh maanane vaale kanoon ko nahin palata he
 However, the Supreme Court has said that it will review section 377

 is prakiya ko certification kaha jaataa haior isamen kisi bhi utpaada kii quality, visheshta or parformens ko certifoi kiya jaataa he
 Whenever you buy goods, make sure to check the standard marks mentioned below for complete information and quality of the product
 is tarah aap shopping main kabhi dhokhaa nahin khaaenge
 ISI- You must have often heard that while shopping, you must see the ISI mark on the product
 ISI mark darasal industrial products kii gunvattta bataane ke liye hota he
 For selling goods in India, he / she must be ISI certified

 sabhi jewelri ke nichle hisse main ek nishaan bana hota he jo yah pruf karata he ki is jewelri kii purity kii guarantee sarkaar le rahi he

 Hardly anyone can deny that those who use public toilets are always at risk of infection
 public toilet kaa istemaal karnaa sehat ke liye khatarnaak ho saktaa he kyonki in toilets main kai tarah ke bacteria hone kii ashanka bahut adhik hoti he

 adhyayanon kii maane to public toilet main hepatitis e, i coli, stryptococus jaise rogaanuon ke maujuud hone kii ashanka bahut adhik hoti he
 In such a situation, try to use public toilet at least and if there is no other option then use clean toilet
